  <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>I am a wedding and lifestyle portrait photographer with more than ten years of experience photographing, what I like to call, “life happening.”
I am passionate about capturing celebrations and milestones in people’s lives. Based in the San Francisco Bay Area, I am fortunate to photograph at stunning locations across California and beyond. My photography style is candid, timeless, romantic, and lighthearted, with an editorial influence. My clients often describe my images as sensitive, genuine, intimate, and spontaneous. My affinity for natural light and organic details allows me to incorporate elements of the surrounding environment into my photography—a soft fern blurring into the foreground, or ancient redwoods framing kissing lovers.
In 2003, I photographed my first wedding in the Sierra National Forest for a dear friend. Guests waded through the creek bed with drinks in hand. The bride and groom exchanged promises on a solitary patch of earth. The bride’s father’s eyes welled with tears and her grandmother’s weathered hands held her bouquet for safekeeping. I knew then that the greatest gift I can give others is to capture images of their most precious occasions. As a result, at the core of my philosophy lies my passion for story-telling and capturing moments that cannot be staged.
I believe in true love, laughing out loud, including everyone, living in the moment, small acts of kindness, the magic of simple things, holding hands, traveling to foreign lands, and singing your heart out to your favorite songs.
Your life story is unique. My goal as a photographer is to illustrate who you are, the interesting parts of your relationship, the arch of emotions that build your story, life’s authenticity and the profound experiences that shape who we are.<span class="more-links"><a title="Read More about Christine Glebov Photography" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDesc(this)">Read more</a></span></p>

  <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>Uzma’s USA is a premier Indian-owned business specializing in luxury Indian wedding photography, cinematic videography, and exquisite bridal makeup services across the United States. Founded by Uzma, a passionate creative with years of experience capturing South Asian weddings, the business brings artistry, cultural depth, and elegance to every event.

With a commitment to storytelling, Uzma’s team transforms each celebration into timeless memories — blending vibrant visuals, emotional candid shots, and stunning bridal portraits. From pre-wedding shoots and sangeet nights to bridal makeup and full wedding cinematography, every service is tailored to reflect the couple’s unique love story and cultural traditions.

Uzma’s USA is also renowned for its bridal makeup artistry, combining traditional beauty with modern glamour to create flawless, radiant looks that last all day. The team’s attention to detail, high-quality products, and expert techniques ensure every bride feels confident, camera-ready, and stunning on her special day.

Whether it’s photography, video, or makeup — Uzma’s USA delivers a one-stop wedding experience that celebrates Indian heritage with contemporary sophistication.<span class="more-links"><a title="Read More about Uzma's USA - Indian Wedding Photography, Video And Indian Bridal Makeup" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDesc(this)">Read more</a></span></p>

  <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>Photography has been my hobby since the digital camera revolution started. I have been clicking pictures since I purchased my first digital camera in 2000 and then D-SLR changed how I looked through the lens. I love everything about colors, be it the vibrant shades on a popsicle or the plain white of a wedding gown. South Indian biryani is my favorite food. I have been blessed with a lovely family: My beautiful wife, Praveena, and my two great kids, Trinity and Judah.   <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>Welcome to Anusha Chandra Photography – Where Moments Come to Life!
For over a decade, I've immersed myself in the art of photography, fueled by an unbridled passion for freezing moments in time and capturing the essence of people. Based in the sun-kissed landscapes of San Diego, my lens extends its reach to the vibrant communities of San Marcos, Temecula, Menifee, Murrieta, Orange County, and the dynamic energy of Los Angeles.
Photography, for me, is not just a profession; it's a lifelong love affair with the art of storytelling through visuals. Each click of the shutter is an opportunity to weave narratives, to preserve the laughter, the tears, the subtle glances, and the grand celebrations that make life truly extraordinary. In the diverse tapestry of Southern California, I find inspiration in the every day and the extraordinary. From the golden beaches to the urban skylines, my camera is a faithful companion, ready to document the unique stories that unfold against the backdrop of this stunning region. At Anusha Chandra Photography, we specialize in not just freezing moments but crafting visual tales that resonate with emotion. Whether it's a housewarming event, a birthday party,  a family portrait session, a Newborn or a maternity shoot, or any event, our lens is attuned to the nuances that make each occasion special. Our expertise extends beyond photography, embracing the dynamic world of videography to bring your moments to life in motion.<span class="more-links"><a title="Read More about Anusha Chandra&nbsp;Photography" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDesc(this)">Read more</a></span></p>

  <div class="description" id="showFullDesc">
    <p>I am drawn to quiet moments. I think it originated from attempts at self-preservation when I was living in neighborhoods that were...difficult. At the age of 7, I built a sanctuary in my room. In this tiny space, I had a large red tent on my bed which rested against the wall furthest from the window because stones had been thrown through it on several occasions. The bed was surrounded by a moat of blankets and my stuffed animals were my guardians. My imagination soared as I created a beautiful, safe haven. The feeling of loneliness drifted away and was replaced by the comfort of solitude. Here is where I found my quiet moments. To this day I still look for the glimpses of quiet when the world is turbulent. These images are a window into my world.    <span class="more-links"><a title="Read More about Nirav Patel Editorial Photographer" href="javascript:void()" onclick="javascript:openFullDesc(this)">Read more</a></span></p>
